<script>
    (function(require){
      require(['modules/01-topNav.min'], function(topNav){
        topNav();

var $location = window.location.origin;
var getCartInfomation = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": $location + "/b2c/eshop/getShoppingCart",
    "method": "GET",
   
    "processData": false,
};

$.ajax(getCartInfomation).done(function(response) {
    if(response.numberOfItemsInCart == 0) {
      $('.badge-top').addClass('hidden');
    }else {
      $('.badge-top').html(response.numberOfItemsInCart);
      $('.badge-top').removeClass('hidden');
    }
  
}).error(function(data) {
});
function updateQueryStringParam(key, value) {
    baseUrl = [location.protocol, '//', location.host, location.pathname].join('');
    urlQueryString = document.location.search;
    var newParam = key + '=' + value,
        params = '?' + newParam;

    if (urlQueryString) {
        keyRegex = new RegExp('([\?&])' + key + '[^&]*');
      
        if (urlQueryString.match(keyRegex) !== null) {
            params = urlQueryString.replace(keyRegex, "$1" + newParam);
        } else {
            params = urlQueryString + '&' + newParam;
        }
    }
    return baseUrl + params;
}

window.changeLangAction = function() {
    var currnetURL = window.location.href;
    var currentLang = $('html').attr('lang');
    var paramName = 'locale';
    if (currnetURL.indexOf('/eshop/') > 0) {
        if (currentLang == 'en' || currentLang == 'EN') {
            newURLEShop = updateQueryStringParam(paramName, "AR");
        } else if (currentLang == 'ar' || currentLang == 'AR') {
            newURLEShop = updateQueryStringParam(paramName, "EN");
        }
        window.location.href = newURLEShop;
    } else {
    var getCurrentURL = window.location.href;
        var getIndexForArabic = getCurrentURL.indexOf('/en/');
        var getIndexForEnglish = getCurrentURL.indexOf('/ar/');
        var resultString = '';
        if(getIndexForArabic != -1){
          resultString = getCurrentURL.replace("/en/", "/ar/");
          window.location.href = resultString;
        } else if(getIndexForEnglish != -1) {
          resultString = getCurrentURL.replace("/ar/", "/en/");
          window.location.href = resultString;
        } else {
          return false;
        }
    


    }
}



      });
    }(require))


  </script>

<script>
  (function(require){
    require(['modules/02-main-menu-full-version.min'], function(menu){
      menu();


 var $location = window.location.origin;
 
            var getUserInfomation = {
                "async": true,
                "crossDomain": true,
                "url": $location + "/b2c/getUserInfo.service",
                "method": "POST",
                "headers": {
                    "Content-Type": "application/json",
                    "cache-control": "no-cache"
                },
                "processData": false,
                "data": "{}"
            };
 
            $.ajax(getUserInfomation).done(function (response) {
                var prasedJSON = JSON.parse(response);
                $('.loginUserPanel').text(prasedJSON["login"]);
                $('.signInLink').addClass('hidden');
                $('.signOutLink').removeClass('hidden');
                loggedInToggle();
        
            }).error(function (data) {
                $('.loginUserPanel').text('MY ACCOUNT');
                $('.signInLink').removeClass('hidden');
                $('.signOutLink').addClass('hidden');
            });
 
 
$(".signOutAction").on('click', function(e) {
var settingsUserLogOut = {
   "async": true,
   "crossDomain": true,
   "url": $location + "/b2c/logoutUser.service",
   "method": "POST",
   "headers": {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "cache-control": "no-cache"
   },
   "processData": false,
   "data": "{}"
  };
$.ajax(settingsUserLogOut).done(function(responseLogout) {
   localStorage.clear();
   $('.loginUserPanel').text('MY ACCOUNT');
   $('.signInLink').removeClass('hidden');
   $('.signOutLink').addClass('hidden');
  $('.account-link').removeClass('active');
  }).fail(function(data) {});
});





          
        if(window.location.href.indexOf("/mobile/") > -1) 
       {
            $('.navbar-left li#dtsecondlevelmenu-1').addClass('active'); 
            $('#dtsecondlevelmenumob-1').addClass('active');              
       }
       else if(window.location.href.indexOf("/devices/") > -1) 
       {
            $('.navbar-left li#dtsecondlevelmenu-2').addClass('active');  
            $('#dtsecondlevelmenumob-2').addClass('active');               
       }
       else if(window.location.href.indexOf("/home/") > -1) 
       {
            $('.navbar-left li#dtsecondlevelmenu-3').addClass('active');    
            $('#dtsecondlevelmenumob-3').addClass('active');             
       }
       else
       {
          $('.navbar-left li').removeClass('active');          
          $('.panel-heading a').removeClass('active');       
       }
       
       if(window.location.href.indexOf("/mobile/plans/") > -1)   
      {
         $('.sub-account-menu li#dtthirdlevelmenu-1').addClass('active');   
         $('#dtthirdlevelmenumob-1').addClass('active');  
      }
      else if(window.location.href.indexOf("/mobile/addons/") > -1)   
      {
        $('.sub-account-menu li#dtthirdlevelmenu-2').addClass('active');   
        $('#dtthirdlevelmenumob-2').addClass('active');  
      }

      if(window.location.href.indexOf("/devices/mobiledevices/") > -1)   
      {
         $('.sub-account-menu li#dtthirdlevelmenu-3').addClass('active');  
         $('#dtthirdlevelmenumob-3').addClass('active');   
      }
      else if(window.location.href.indexOf("/devices/homedevices/") > -1)   
      {
        $('.sub-account-menu li#dtthirdlevelmenu-4').addClass('active');   
        $('#dtthirdlevelmenumob-4').addClass('active');  
      }
     /* else if(window.location.href.indexOf("/devices/smartliving/") > -1)   
      {
        $('.sub-account-menu li#dtthirdlevelmenu-5').addClass('active');   
      } */
      if(window.location.href.indexOf("/home/plans/") > -1)   
      {
         $('.sub-account-menu li#dtthirdlevelmenu-5').addClass('active');   
         $('#dtthirdlevelmenumob-5').addClass('active');  
      }
      else if(window.location.href.indexOf("/home/addons/") > -1)   
      {
        $('.sub-account-menu li#dtthirdlevelmenu-6').addClass('active');  
        $('#dtthirdlevelmenumob-6').addClass('active');

        success : function(res) {
          var productRow = 'productsRow-' + payload.categoryId;
          var htmlCards = getProductCard(res);
          $('#' + productRow).html(htmlCards);
          if("Carousal"=="Carousal") {
            if ($('.swiper-slide').length > 3){
              $('.swiper-scrollbar').removeClass('hide');
              $('.table-swiper-button-prev').removeClass('hide');
              $('.table-swiper-button-next').removeClass('hide');
              cards();
            }
          } else {
            $('#' + productRow).removeClass('swiper-wrapper');
            if ($('#' + productRow  +' .swiper-slide').length > 6){
      $('#' + productRow  +' .swiper-slide').closest('.related-products').next().removeClass('hide');
               /*$('.load-btn').removeClass('hide');*/
              $('#' + productRow +' .swiper-slide').each(function(i){
                if (i >= 6){
                  $(this).addClass('hide')
                }
              });
              $('#' + productRow).closest('.content-section').find('.load-btn .btn').unbind().on('click', function(e){
                e.preventDefault();
                $(this).closest('.content-section').find('.swiper-slide').removeClass('hide');
                $(this).parent().addClass('hide');
              });
            }
          }
          /*google*/
          $(function(){
                    var allProductImpressions = {
                    'event': 'productImpressions',
                    'ecommerce': {
                        'currencyCode': 'AED',
                        'impressions': []
                      }
                    };
                    var productDetails = $('#'+productRow).children('.swiper-slide');
                    $(productDetails).each(function( index ) {
                        var productImpration = {}
                        var selectedProductMain = $(this).find('.tiles-box');
                        var name = selectedProductMain.find('.tiles-box-title').find('h2').text();
                        var brand = selectedProductMain.find('.tiles-box-title').find('.catagory').text();
                        var price = selectedProductMain.find('.tiles-box-list').find('.price').text();
                        var position = $(this).index()+1;
                        var curnt =  selectedProductMain.find('a').attr('href');
                        var category = getParameterByName('catName',curnt);
                        var id = getParameterByName('productId',curnt);
                        productImpration = {
                          'name':          name,            /*String - Product Name*/
                          'id':            id,           /*String - Product ID*/
                          'price':         price,                 /*String - Product Price*/

             var productClickedDetails = $('#'+productRow).children('.swiper-slide').find('a');
             $(productClickedDetails).unbind().on('click',function(e){

     function getParameterByName(name, url) {
          if (!url) url = window.location.href;
          name = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, '\$&');
          var regex = new RegExp('[?&]' + name + '(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)'),
              results = regex.exec(url);
          if (!results) return null;
          if (!results[2]) return '';
          return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
      }
    var numberWithCommas = function(x) {
      x = x.toString();
      var pattern = /(-?\d+)(\d{3})/;
      while (pattern.test(x))
        x = x.replace(pattern, "$1,$2");
      return x;
  }
     function getProductCard(data){
        var products = data.products;
        var html = '';
        var featuredTile = $('.product-grid-cms');
        var featuredPosition = 0;
		var promoText = 'SPECIAL OFFER ';
		var off =" % OFF";
		if (window.location.href.indexOf("/ar/") > -1){
			promoText = ' عرض خاص ';
			off =" % أقل ";
		}
        if (featuredTile.length){
          featuredPosition = featuredTile.data('position');
        }
        for (var i = 0; i<products.length; i++){
          if (featuredPosition == i + 1){
            html += '<div class="swiper-slide col-xs-12 col-sm-6 col-md-4">';
            html += featuredTile.html();
            html += '</div>'
          }
          var product = products[i];
          var classes = 'tile-table device-card';
      var redirectUrl = '/b2c/eshop/device-configuration?productId=' +product.productId+ '&catName=' +"Smartphones";
          if (product.oldPrice){
            classes = 'tile-table device-card offer'
          }
          html += '<div class="swiper-slide col-xs-12 col-sm-6 col-md-4">' +
                '<div class="'+classes+'">' +
                  '<div class="tile-card effect__click">' +
                      '<a href="'+ redirectUrl +'" class="tile">' +
                          '<div class="tile-card__front">' +
                              '<div class="tiles-box content body-standard">' +
                                  '<div class="product">' +
                                      '<img class="product-img" src="'+ product.image +'" alt="device">' +
                                  '</div>' +
                                  '<div class="tiles-box-title">';
          if (product.oldPrice != undefined && product.oldPrice > 0){
            html +=                 '<div class="special-offer">'+ promoText+ parseFloat((product.oldPrice - product.price)/product.price*100).toFixed(2) + off+'</div>';
          }
          html +=                   '<div class="catagory">'+product.brand+'</div>' +
                                      '<h2 dir="ltr">'+product.productName+'</h2>' +
                                      '<ul class="colorList">';
          if (product.hasOwnProperty('availableConfgiurations')){
            var config = product.availableConfgiurations;
            for (var j = 0; j < config.length; j++){
                if (config[j].type === 'COLOR'){
                  html += '<li style="background-color:'+ config[j].value +'">'+ config[j].name +'</li>';
              }
            }
          }
          var buyNowText = "BUY NOW";
          if (product.isPreorder){
            buyNowText = "Pre-order";
          }
          var aedText = " AED ";
          var fromText = " From ";
          var wasText = " was ";
          var vatText = " 5% VAT excluded";
      var or = "or ";
      var smilePoints = " Smiles Points"
      if (window.location.href.indexOf("/ar/") > -1){
      redirectUrl = redirectUrl + '&locale=AR';
      buyNowText = "اشترِ الآن";
            if (product.isPreorder){
                buyNowText = "اطلبه مسبقًا";
            }
            var wasText = " كان ";
            aedText = " درهم ";
            fromText = " بدءا من ";
            vatText = " غير متضمن 5% ضريبة القيمة المضافة ";
      or = " أو ";
      smilePoints = " نقاط بسمات "
      }
          html +=                     '</ul>' +
                                  '</div>' +
                                  '<div class="tiles-box-list auto">' +
                                      '<div class="detail-info-wrap detail-info-wrap-pricetag">' +
                                          '<div class="detail-price-new">' +
                                              '<div class="main-part">' +
                                                  '<div dir="ltr" class="from">'+ fromText +'</div>';
          if (product.discountPrice != '' && product.discountPrice > 0){
            html += '<div dir="ltr" class="price">'+ parseFloat(product.discountPrice).toFixed(2) +' </div>';
          } else {
            html += '<div dir="ltr" class="price">'+ parseFloat(product.price).toFixed(2) +' </div>';
          }
          html +=                               '<small>'+ aedText +'</small>' +
                                              '</div>' +
                                          '</div>' +
                                      '</div>';
            html += '<p class="bottom-text">' ;
      if (product.oldPrice != '' && product.oldPrice > 0){
                    html +=     '<span class="before-price-container">'+ wasText +' <span class="before-price">'+parseInt(product.oldPrice).toFixed(2)+ aedText + ' </span></span>' ;
      }               
          html += vatText +'</p>';
          html +=               '</div>';
      html +=           '<div class="smile-points">'+or+ numberWithCommas(parseInt(product.price)*100) + smilePoints+'</div>'  +
              '<a href="'+ redirectUrl +'"><div class="read-more select-product-from-grid select-product-from-grid-without-close" data-extra-container=".extra-options-02">' +
                                '<span>'+ buyNowText  +'</span>' +
                                '</div></a>' +
                              '</div>' +
                          '</div>' +
                      '</a>' +
                  '</div>' +
              '</div>' +
            '</div>';
        }
        return html;
      }
    });
  }(require))

      function getPlansCard(data) {
                        var products = data.products;
                        var html = '';
                        for (var i = 0; i < products.length; i++) {
                            var product = products[i];
                            var classes = 'tile-table plan-card';

                            var offer = false;
                            if (sku.promoText != undefined)
                                offer = true;
                            if (offer) {
                                classes = 'tile-table plan-card offer'
                            }

                            else if(plantype.value.indexOf('Shop')!== -1)
                            {
                                var redirectUrl = document.getElementById('redurlpreprod').value+'productId=' + product.productId + '&skuId=' + sku.skuId + '&catName='+ "Postpaid_plan";
                            }
                            else if(plantype.value.indexOf('Create Your Number')!== -1)
                            {
                                var redirectUrl =document.getElementById('redurlpreprod').value+ '&catName='+ "Postpaid_plan";
                            }
                            else if(plantype.value.indexOf('Call Back Auto')!== -1)
                            {
                                var redirectUrl =document.getElementById('redurlpreprod').value;
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                var redirectUrl = document.getElementById('redurlpreprod').value+'productId=' + product.productId + '&skuId=' + sku.skuId + '&catName='+ "Postpaid_plan";
                            }
                            html += '<div class="swiper-slide col-xs-12 col-sm-6 col-md-4">' +
                                '<div class="' + classes + '">' +
                                '<div class="tile-card effect__click">' ;
                             if (sku.vasIsEligibleForAccountType != undefined){
                                html += '<a href="'+redirectUrl+'" class="tile '+ sku.vasIsEligibleForAccountType.toLocaleLowerCase() +'">' ;
                              }else{
                                html +=  '<a href="'+redirectUrl+'" class="tile ">' ;
                              }
                             html +=  '<div class="tile-card__front">' +
                                '<div class="tiles-box content body-standard">' +
                                '<div class="tiles-box-title">';
                            if (offer) {
                                html += '<div class="special-offer">' + sku.promoText + '</div>';
                            }
                            html += '<div class="catagory">' + product.productName + '</div>' +
                                '<h2>' + sku.displayName + '</h2>' +
                                '</div>' +
                                '<div class="tiles-box-list">' +
                                '<ul class="featureList">';
							var buyNowText = "BUY NOW";
                            var aedText = " AED ";
                            var vatText = " 5% VAT excluded";
							var validityType = ''
                            if(window.location.href.indexOf("/ar/") > -1){
                                dynamicAttributes = sku.dynamicAttributesArList;
                                redirectUrl = redirectUrl + '&locale=AR';
                                buyNowText = "اشترِ الآن";
                                aedText = " درهم ";
                                vatText = " غير متضمن 5% ضريبة القيمة المضافة ";
                            }
                            for (var j = 0; j < dynamicAttributes.length; j++) {
                                html += '<li>' + dynamicAttributes[j].value  + '</li>';
                            }
                            html += '</ul>' +
                                '<div class="detail-info-wrap detail-info-wrap-pricetag">' +
                                '<div class="detail-price-new">' +
                                '<div class="main-part">';
                            if (offer) {
                                html += '<div dir="ltr" class="price">' + parseFloat(sku.discountPrice ).toFixed(2) + '</div>';
                            } else {
                                html += '<div dir="ltr" class="price">' + parseFloat(sku.listPrice).toFixed(2) + '</div>'
                            }
							if(sku.validityType){
								validityType = '/'+sku.validityType;
							} 
                            html += '<small>'+ aedText + validityType+'</small>' +
                                '</div>' +
                                '</div>' +
                                '</div>' +
                                '<p class="bottom-text">';
                            if (offer) {
                                html += '<span class="before-price-container">was <span class="before-price">' +  parseFloat(sku.listPrice).toFixed(2) + aedText +' </span></span>';
                            }
                            html += vatText +
                                '</p>' +
                                '</div>';
              html += '<a href="'+ redirectUrl +'"><div class="read-more select-product-from-grid select-product-from-grid-without-close" data-extra-container=".extra-options-02">' +
                                '<span>'+buyNowText +'</span>' +
                                '</div></a>' +
                                '</div>' +
                                '</div>' +
                                '</a>' +
                                '</div>' +
                                '</div> ' +
                                '</div>';
                        }
                        return html;
                    }
                    function getParameterByName(name, url) {
                        if (!url) url = window.location.href;
                        name = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, '\$&');
                        var regex = new RegExp('[?&]' + name + '(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)'),
                            results = regex.exec(url);
                        if (!results) return null;
                        if (!results[2]) return '';
                        return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
                    }
    });
  }(require))
